\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{new\_settrie()}{new\_settrie()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int new\+\_\+settrie (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Create a new \mbox{\hyperlink{classSetTrie}{Set\+Trie}} object that can be used via the Python interface.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A unique ID that can be passed as the st\+\_\+id parameter for any method in the Python interface.
\end{DoxyReturn}
To free the resources allocated by this ID, the (python) caller must call \mbox{\hyperlink{settrie_8cpp_ad5b3d49f3cdac771f72d3f6b7cfb8f88}{destroy\+\_\+settrie()}} with the st\+\_\+id and never use the same st\+\_\+id after that. \mbox{\Hypertarget{py__settrie__wrap_8cpp_a68241c91262da8c0dcb681eb827ec1ac}\label{py__settrie__wrap_8cpp_a68241c91262da8c0dcb681eb827ec1ac}}

On error, it will return -\/3 if the st\+\_\+id or the set\+\_\+id is invalid and -\/2 if the set\+\_\+id given is the last set in the object or the object is empty.
